# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
To differentiate implicitly you only need to know 2 things:
- Differentiate each side of the equation (using chain rule, product or quotient if necessary)
- Remember that y differentiated with respect to x is by definition dy/dx ^rFgjC6CO

Find the value of dy/dx at the point (1,1), where ^6oP9lUg4

A curve is described by the equation

a) Find the coordinates of the two points on the curve where x = -8. (3)
b) Find the gradient of the curve at each of these points. (6) ^fPgVaDwn
